Typically hard money lenders will lend 50-70% of the value of the property regardless of the sales price (unlike banks). The first step of the foreclosure process (which typically takes a number of months) that the lender will take is to file the notice of default. This is a public document that is recorded.\r\n* Tax liens - Each state creates the system and rules for the lien or deed process so careful research is necessary. In general, property owners are notified regarding the amount of taxes owed and are given a period of time to pay.\r\n* Wholesaling - Wholesalers typically make smaller profits but buy and sell properties in large quantities. Your current reservation status will be shown instantly.\r\nPNR is a 10 digit number, usually printed on top-left corner of your Indian Railway's counter ticket. If you have booked your ticket from IRCTC, then you can find this number on your electronically generated E-tickets. Also, IRCTC sends an SMS on your mobile phone in which all the necessary details regarding ticket is present. This booking SMS from IRCTC includes PNR number. You can locate it and use it to find current reservation status of your ticket.\r\nHow to check time table of different trains?\r\nIndian Railways run thousands of trains daily. In order to check train schedule using Trainspnrstatus app, open this app and click on menu icon present in top right corner of the display. Once you click menu, it will show different links of the sections. Simply click on 'Train Schedule' option. Enter five digit train number and hit get train schedule button. After successful submission of train number, app will show you detailed time table of that train. From starting station to ending station, all scheduled time of trains are listed in table in chronological order for better understanding. \r\nNow if you need to check live train status, all you need to do is to select station and running days information from the available form on top. Clicking submit button will load live running status information about a train.\r\nAnother great feature of this app is that it can provide you the list of all trains running between two important stations. After selecting 'Trains Between Stations' options, enter details of 'from' and 'to' in the form. Click 'Get Trains Between' button. It will load all the trains with departure and arrival time. It will also list train running days information. Distance between those two station and travel time will also be listed for better understanding.\r\nApart from main features of Trainspnrstatus app like PNR Status, train schedule and live status; one
